     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <h1 class="page-header">State Governmental Relations</h1> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <ul class="nav nav-tabs sub-nav tab6"> 
        <li class="active"><a class="" href="index.html">Overview</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="staff-liaisons/index.html">Staff &amp; Liaisons</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="legislation/index.html">Legislation</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="budget/index.html">Budget</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="advocacy/index.html">Advocacy</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="resources/index.html">Resources</a></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- Example row of columns --> 
     <div class="row-fluid"> 
      <div class="span4 hero-unit"> 
       <p>We serve as the primary university representative to state elected officials and agencies.</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4">
       <p>State Governmental Relations (SGR)&nbsp;serves to advance understanding and support for UC's tripartite mission of teaching, research and public service. As UC's principal representative to state elected officials and state agencies in Sacramento, we represent university positions on legislative, budgetary and policy matters.</p>
      </div> 
      <div class="span4"> 
       <div class="row-fluid dotted-bottom"> 
        <div class="span4 dept-head"> 
         <img alt="Steve Juarez" src="_files/steve-juarez.jpg" />
        </div> 
        <div class="span8"> 
         <p class="blue"> Steve Juarez </p> 
         <p>Associate Vice President &amp; Director</p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row-fluid"> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon staff" href="staff-liaisons/index.html">Staff Directory</a>
        </div> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon org" href="_files/sgr-org-chart.pdf">Org Chart</a>
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div>

    ytpreload.getSnapClass = function(guidePinned) {
      var SCROLLBAR_WIDTH = 21;
      var CONTENT_PADDING = 50;
      var GUIDE_WIDTH = 230;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_2 = 1056;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_3 = 1262;
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;

      var spaceForContent = screenWidth - SCROLLBAR_WIDTH - CONTENT_PADDING;
      if (ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle() && guidePinned) {
        spaceForContent -= GUIDE_WIDTH;
      }

      if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_3) {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[2];
      } else if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_2){
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[1];
      } else {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[0];
      }

    };
    ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS = 'guide-pinned';
    ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS = 'show-guide';

      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;
      return screenWidth >= 1251;

        // Google WaterMark Script
        $(function () {
            $("#txtGoogleSearch").each(function () {
                ToggleHint($(this)); // add class on page load to elements with "hintable" class
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").focus(function () {
                $(this).removeClass("GoogleWatermark"); // handle all focus hints
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").blur(function () {
                ToggleHint(this); // handle all blur hints
            });
        });

        function ToggleHint(obj) {
            if ($(obj).val() == '') { $(obj).addClass("GoogleWatermark"); };
        }
    </script>

     <img src="/Images/finals.png" alt="" class="page-lead" /> 
     <div class="span-18 last"> 
      <h3>Plan For Your Final Exams</h3> 
      <p>Use these tables to find out when your finals take place. Most final times are based on class meeting times, but some will combine multiple sections or take place during special time blocks.</p> 
      <ul class="orange-bullets wide" style="margin-bottom: 30px;"> 
       <li>Its up to you to plan your class schedule so that your final exams dont conflict.</li> 
       <li>If your regular class meeting time changes during the quarter, that means your final exam time changes, too. The time of your final will be based on the new class meeting time, not the original.</li> 
       <li>Although most finals are held in the same room where class is held, some finals may take place in an alternative classroom. Check with your instructor for the location of your exam.</li> 
       <li>Types of final exams vary  your final might be a term paper, an in-class written or oral exam, a take-home test or some other method of evaluation. Talk to your instructor about what to expect.</li> 
       <li>Written final exams will not exceed three hours.</li> 
       <li>Read our <a href="../../Content/pdfs/religious_accommodation_policy.pdf" target="_blank">Policy on Religious Accommodation</a> if you are worried about finals conflicting with religious observances.</li> 
      </ul> 
     </div>

  <div class="pagewrapper"> 
   <h3 class="accessibility">Footer</h3> 
   <div id="colophon">
     The University of California, Riverside (
    <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/">www.ucr.edu</a>) is a doctoral research university, a living laboratory for groundbreaking exploration of issues critical to Inland Southern California, the state and communities around the world. Reflecting California's diverse culture, UCR's enrollment has exceeded 21,000 students. The campus opened a medical school in 2013 and has reached the heart of the Coachella Valley by way of the UCR Palm Desert Center. The campus has an annual statewide economic impact of more than $1 billion. A broadcast studio with fiber cable to the AT&amp;T Hollywood hub is available for live or taped interviews. UCR also has ISDN for radio interviews. To learn more, call (951) UCR-NEWS. 
   </div>
